## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start: is_within_expected] --> B{eta_range_min exists?}
    B -->|Yes| C{actualEta >= min?}
    B -->|No| D{eta_range_max exists?}
    C -->|No| E[Return DriftWarning: below min]
    C -->|Yes| D
    D -->|Yes| F{actualEta <= max?}
    D -->|No| G{expected_eta & threshold exist?}
    F -->|No| H[Return DriftWarning: above max]
    F -->|Yes| G
    G -->|Yes| I{within threshold?}
    G -->|No| J[Return None]
    I -->|No| K[Return DriftWarning: threshold exceeded]
    I -->|Yes| J
    E --> L[End]
    H --> L
    K --> L
    J --> L
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start: test_event] --> B[Call lambda_handler with query_string_params]
    B --> C[Parse response]
    C --> D{statusCode == 200?}
    D -->|No| E[Assert Failure]
    D -->|Yes| F{etaCalculation exists?}
    F -->|No| G[Assert Failure]
    F -->|Yes| H{was_override?}
    H -->|Yes| I[Skip validation - Return]
    H -->|No| J{expected_data exists?}
    J -->|No| I
    J -->|Yes| K[Call expected_data.is_within_expected]
    K --> L{drift_warning?}
    L -->|Yes| M[Warn about drift]
    L -->|No| N[Test passes]
    M --> N
    E --> O[End]
    I --> O
    N --> O
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant T as Test Runner
    participant TF as test_event
    participant LH as lambda_handler
    participant ED as ExpectedData
    participant DW as DriftWarning
    T->>TF: Execute test with params
    TF->>LH: Invoke with query_string_params
    LH-->>TF: Return response dict
    TF->>TF: Assert statusCode == 200
    TF->>TF: Parse JSON body
    TF->>TF: Check if override used
    alt Override used or no expected_data
        TF->>T: Return (skip validation)
    else Validate expected data
        TF->>ED: is_within_expected(response_json)
        ED->>ED: Check eta_range_min
        ED->>ED: Check eta_range_max
        ED->>ED: Check threshold
        alt Drift detected
            ED->>DW: Create DriftWarning
            DW-->>ED: Return warning
            ED-->>TF: Return warning
            TF->>TF: Warn about drift
        else No drift
            ED-->>TF: Return None
        end
        TF->>T: Test complete
    end
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> InitTest
    InitTest --> InvokeLambda: Setup params
    InvokeLambda --> ValidateResponse: Get response
    ValidateResponse --> CheckStatusCode: Parse JSON
    CheckStatusCode --> Failed: statusCode != 200
    CheckStatusCode --> CheckEtaField: statusCode == 200
    CheckEtaField --> Failed: etaCalculation missing
    CheckEtaField --> CheckOverride: etaCalculation exists
    CheckOverride --> Complete: Override used
    CheckOverride --> CheckExpectedData: ML result
    CheckExpectedData --> Complete: No expected_data
    CheckExpectedData --> ValidateDrift: expected_data exists
    ValidateDrift --> WarnDrift: Drift detected
    ValidateDrift --> Complete: No drift
    WarnDrift --> Complete
    Complete --> [*]
    Failed --> [*]
```
